Mass Provisioning Attributes Documentation

Mass Provisioning Command Attributes Documentation

Types

The following types are supported:

  • bool= [0,1,false,true]
  • string= [_a-zA-Z0-9.-:?!#$%^&*()+|{}][][ /_a-zA-Z0-9.-:?!#$%^&*()+|{};][]*]
  • integer = [-2,147,483,648 to 2,147,483,647]
  • enum= [See specific values below]

Provisioning Commands

ABM

BGNAME:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-30) Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"The name of the Business Group"
BGMAINNUMBER:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-30) Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"The Main number associated with the BG"
BGMAINNUMBERATTENDANT:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-30) Default:""
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The attendant number"
AUTOATTENDANTNUMBER:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-30) Default:""
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The auto attendant number"
AUTOATTENDANTSTATUS:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[Enabled Disabled]" Default:"Disabled"
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The status for the auto attendant number"

CfAcctCode

ENABLED:
    Type:bool
    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Whether the service is active"

CFACR

ENABLED:
    Type:bool
    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates wheter the feature is active or not"
SUBCONTROLLED:
    Type:bool
    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates whether the subscriber can enable/disable the feature or whether it is controlled by the telco only"
BILLING:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[FlatRate Usagesensitive]" Default:"FlatRate"
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates type of billing"

APAC

NUMBERPLANNAME:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-31) Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"Name of Number Plan"
DIGITS:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-24) Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"Prefix Access Code"
DNMINLEN:
    Type:int
    Values:(min:0 max:30) Default:0
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The minimum lenght of the digits used for digit matching"
DNMAXLEN:
    Type:int
    Values:(min:0 max:30) Default:0
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The maximum lenght of the digits used for digit matching"
PREFIXTYPE:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[PAC_Operator0Plus PAC_Operator0 PAC_Operator00 PAC_OperatorIntl PAC_FGD PAC_IDD PAC_DDD PAC_NoPrefix PAC_VerticalSvcCode PAC_SpeedCode PAC_CarrierCode PAC_InvalidCode_ PAC_Extension PAC_OffNetAc PAC_OnNetAc PAC_FacilityAc PAC_AttendantAc PAC_HomeCarrierCode PAC_HomeNRN PAC_PreventINTriggering PAC_ServiceCode PAC_SatelliteAvoidance PAC_CircuitSwitchedData PAC_HotlineVoiceGrade PAC_HotlineDataGrade]" Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"Indicates the type of prefix and access code"
DIGITPOS:
    Type:int
    Values:- Default:0
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates the number of leading digits to be stripped  from Destination DN before translating the resulting DN"
DIGITSINSERT:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-15) Default:""
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates the number of leading digits to be stripped from the destination DN before translating the resulting DN"
TRAILINGDIGITPOS:
    Type:int
    Values:(min:0 max:30) Default:30
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates the position at which to delete extraneous trailing digits"
NOA:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[PAC_Unknown PAC_Subscriber PAC_National PAC_International PAC_PrefixBased PAC_NoDn PAC_L0 PAC_L1 PAC_L2 PAC_NoaExtension PAC_PrefixBasedNoTNS PAC_NRN_CPN]" Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"Indicates the Nature of Address of the DN resulting from the digit editing"
DESTTYPE:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[PAC_Undefined PAC_Dest PAC_Service PAC_InvalidCode PAC_E164Dest PAC_BGCommonDest PAC_LocalToll]" Default:"PAC_Undefined"
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Type of Destination"
DESTNAME:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-15) Default:""
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates the name of the destination"
CACLENGTH:
    Type:int
    Values:(min:0 max:6) Default:0
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates the length of the Carrier Access Code (CAC) after the digit position"

    Type:bool
    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Feature is active or not"
ONSTYPE:
    Type:enum
    Values:"[InboundAndOutbound]" Default:"InboundAndOutbound"
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"The type of ONS service to be provided"
STATICONDACTIVATE:
    Type:bool
    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
    Comment:"Indicates whether the Static OND feature is active or not"
STATICONDSERVICEID:
    Type:string
    Length:(1-15) Default:-
    Mandatory:yes
    Comment:"The Preferred device target for ONS binding on inbound calls"

    Default:false
    Mandatory:no
